## **WorldCafe** 

### Publications {#publications}

* [The World Cafe Book: Shaping Our Futures Through Conversations that Matter](http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1576753565/ref=as_li_tf_tl?ie=UTF8&tag=theworldcafe-20&linkCode=as2&camp=1789&creative=9325&creativeASIN=1576753565) by Juanita Brown and David Isaacs with the World Café Community of Practice

* [The Art of Powerful Questions](http://www.theworldcafe.com/tools-store/store/) This comprehensive guide written by Eric Vogt, Juanita Brown and David Isaacs explores the three dimensions of a powerful question–construction, scope and assumptions–and then offers sample questions for focusing collective attention, finding deeper insight and creating forward movement.

* [The World Cafe Resource Guide](http://www.theworldcafe.com/tools-store/store/). In this beautifully illustrated booklet, Juanita Brown, Nancy Margulies and the World Café Community articulate seven guiding principles for you to use in hosting your own World Café. Learn how to craft powerful questions, understand the assumptions and etiquette behind successful World Cafés, & more\!

* [The World Café: Living Knowledge Through Conversations That Matter](http://www.theworldcafe.com/tools-store/store/) In this reprint of her breakthrough doctoral dissertation, Juanita Brown describes the “birth” of the World Café and her own intellectual journey in discovering the power of conversation for accessing collective intelligence, building new knowledge, and bringing forth desired futures.

* [The World Café: Shaping Our Futures Through Conversations that Matter](http://www.theworldcafe.com/global-impact/world-cafe-book/) An award-winning best-seller by Juanita Brown, David Isaacs and the World Café Community, published by Berrett-Koehler, 2005 *(currently translated into nine languages: Spanish, Portuguese, Turkish, Japanese, Simple Chinese, Complex Chinese, German, Korean, and Thai – see link for details)*

* [Conversational Leadership: Thinking Together for a Change](http://www.theworldcafe.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/07/Conversational-Leadership.pdf)  by Thomas J Hurley and Juanita Brown, from The Systems Thinker, November 2009

* [The World Café: Living Knowledge Through Conversations That Matter](http://www.theworldcafe.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/07/STCoverStory.pdf).  The Systems Thinker, July 2001

* [Multi-Generational Collaboration: Shaping Tomorrow, Together](http://www.theworldcafe.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/07/KosmosMulti-GenArticle.pdf) by Juanita Brown, David Isaacs, and Samantha Tan, from Kosmos magazine, Volume VII, Number 2

* [Asking Big Questions](http://www.theworldcafe.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/07/askingbig.pdf). By Juanita Brown, David Isaacs and Nancy Margulies. From The Dance Of Change. Peter Senge, et al editors.

* [Strategic Questioning: Engaging People’s Best Thinking](http://www.theworldcafe.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/07/Strategic-Questioning.pdf) By Juanita Brown, David Isaacs, Eric Vogt, and Nancy Margulies. The Systems Thinker, November 2002

* [Building Corporations as Communities: Merging the Best of Two Worlds](http://www.theworldcafe.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/07/mergingbest.pdf) By Juanita Brown and David Isaacs. From The Fifth Discipline Fieldbook, Peter Senge, et.al eds.

* [The World Café: Parts One & Two](http://www.theworldcafe.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/07/WorldCafe.pdf). By Dr Alexander Schieffer, Bo Gyllenpalm and David Issacs. World Business Academy, Transformation: Volume 18, Issue 8, July 2004

* [Conversation As A Core Business Process](http://www.theworldcafe.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/07/CCCBP.pdf). By Juanita Brown and David Isaacs. The Systems Thinker, December/January, 1996/1997.

* [Mindshift: Strategic Dialogue for Breakthrough Thinking](http://www.theworldcafe.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/07/Mindshift.pdf). By Juanita Brown and Sherrin Bennett. From Learning Organizations: Developing Cultures for Tomorrow’s Workplace. S. Chawla and J. Renesch eds.

* [A Virtual Knowledge Café](http://www.theworldcafe.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/07/virtualcafes.pdf). By Bo Gyllenpalm, Fielding Graduate University Faculty, for Whole Systems Associates, 2000\.

* [The Art of Online Hosting](http://www.theworldcafe.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/07/onlinehosting.pdf). By Amy Lenzo and Adriano Pianesi. The Systems Thinker, March 2011\.

* [The World Cafe: We Are Wiser Together](http://www.theworldcafe.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/Interview-with-Amy-Lenzo.pdf) (PDF 417K), Interview with Amy Lenzo, Collaborative Services blog (January, 2014\)

* [Interview with Amy Lenzo](http://www.theworldcafe.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/07/Neuland-WCInterview.pdf), excerpted from Neuland’s Dialog issue dedicated to World Cafe, January 2011

* [Seeds of Knowledge](http://www.theworldcafe.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/07/seeds.pdf) adapted from The Knowledge Evolution: Expanding Organizational Intelligence. By Verna Allee.

* [The World Café: Catalyzing Large-Scale Collective Learning](http://www.theworldcafe.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/07/catalyzinglearning.pdf) By Juanita Brown, David Isaacs, Nancy Margulies and Gary Warhaftig. From Leverage Magazine, published by Pegasus Communications, Cambridge, MA, September 1999\.

### Reading List {#reading-list}

* [Appreciative Inquiry](http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1576753565/ref=as_li_tf_tl?ie=UTF8&tag=theworldcafe-20&linkCode=as2&camp=1789&creative=9325&creativeASIN=1576753565) by David Cooperrider and Diana Whitney  
  Written by the founders of AI, this short, practical guide offers an approach to organizational change based on the possibility of a more positive future.

* [The Art of Convening](http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1605096687/ref=as_li_tf_tl?ie=UTF8&tag=theworldcafe-20&linkCode=as2&camp=1789&creative=9325&creativeASIN=1605096687) by Craig & Patricia Neal, with Cindy Wold  
  Details a powerful set of principles and practices for making any gathering productive, meaningful, and transformative.

* [The Art of Possibility](http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/0142001104/ref=as_li_tf_tl?ie=UTF8&tag=theworldcafe-20&linkCode=as2&camp=1789&creative=9325&creativeASIN=0142001104) by Benjamin Zander and Rosamund Stone Zander  
  Presenting twelve breakthrough practices for bringing creativity into all human endeavors.

* [Artful Leadership](http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1412085780/ref=as_li_tf_tl?ie=UTF8&tag=theworldcafe-20&linkCode=as2&camp=1789&creative=9325&creativeASIN=1412085780) by Michael Jones  
  Aims to empower leadership development and innovation by connecting the world of the performing arts and the business world.

* [Authentic Conversations](http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1576755959/ref=as_li_tf_tl?ie=UTF8&tag=theworldcafe-20&linkCode=as2&camp=1789&creative=9325&creativeASIN=1576755959) by Jamie Showkier and Maren Showkier  
  Authentic Conversations takes a radical new look at the potentially transformational role of workplace conversations.

* [The Back of the Napkin](http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1591843065/ref=as_li_tf_tl?ie=UTF8&tag=theworldcafe-20&linkCode=as2&camp=1789&creative=9325&creativeASIN=1591843065) by Dan Roam  
  Explains how to use visual-thinking tools to solve business problems and convey ideas with little more than a scrap of paper.

* [Calling the Circle](http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/0553379003/ref=as_li_tf_tl?ie=UTF8&tag=theworldcafe-20&linkCode=as2&camp=1789&creative=9325&creativeASIN=0553379003) by Christina Baldwin  
  Christina Baldwin offers this powerful new tool to everyone who longs for a community based on honesty, equality, and spiritual integrity.

* [The Change Handbook](http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1576753794/ref=as_li_tf_tl?ie=UTF8&tag=theworldcafe-20&linkCode=as2&camp=1789&creative=9325&creativeASIN=1576753794%22%3EThe%20Change%20Handbook%3C/a%3E%3Cimg%20src=%22http://www.assoc-amazon.com/e/ir?t=theworldcafe-20&l=as2&o=1&a=1576753794), Eds Peggy Holman, Steven Cady, and Tom Devane  
  This definitive resource invites people and systems to gather around issues that they care about, unleashing the energy and wisdom to move their dreams into action.

* [Community: The Structure of Belonging](http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1605092770/ref=as_li_tf_tl?ie=UTF8&tag=theworldcafe-20&linkCode=as2&camp=1789&creative=9325&creativeASIN=1605092770%22%3ECommunity:%20The%20Structure%20of%20Belonging%3C/a%3E%3Cimg%20src=%22http://www.assoc-amazon.com/e/ir?t=theworldcafe-20&l=as2&o=1&a=1605092770) by Peter Block  
  Offers a way of thinking about our places that creates an opening for authentic communities to exist and details what each of us can do to make that happen.

* [Dialogue: The Art of Thinking Together](http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/0385479999/ref=as_li_tf_tl?ie=UTF8&tag=theworldcafe-20&linkCode=as2&camp=1789&creative=9325&creativeASIN=0385479999) by William Isaacs  
  Provides practical guidelines for one of the essential elements of true partnership–learning how to talk together in honest and effective ways.

* [Digital Habitats](http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/0982503601/ref=as_li_tf_tl?ie=UTF8&tag=theworldcafe-20&linkCode=as2&camp=1789&creative=9325&creativeASIN=0982503601) by Nancy White, Etienne Wenger and John Smith  
  This book develops a new social literacy and language to describe the practice of stewarding technology for communities.

* [Engaging Emergence](http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1605095214/ref=as_li_tf_tl?ie=UTF8&tag=theworldcafe-20&linkCode=as2&camp=1789&creative=9325&creativeASIN=1605095214) by Peggy Holman  
  Shows how to spot the emergence of a new level of order from the seemingly chaotic change and offers practices and principles that will help you align yourself and your organization with the new order.

* [The Facilitative Way](http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/097297640X/ref=as_li_tf_tl?ie=UTF8&tag=theworldcafe-20&linkCode=as2&camp=1789&creative=9325&creativeASIN=097297640X) by Priscilla Wilson  
  The Facilitative Way includes five approaches to working together more effectively.

* [The Fifth Discipline](http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/0385517254/ref=as_li_tf_tl?ie=UTF8&tag=theworldcafe-20&linkCode=as2&camp=1789&creative=9325&creativeASIN=0385517254) by Peter Senge  
  Senge explains why the “learning organization” matters, provides an unvarnished summary of his management principles and offers some basic tools for practicing it.

* [Finding Our Way](http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1576754057/ref=as_li_tf_tl?ie=UTF8&tag=theworldcafe-20&linkCode=as2&camp=1789&creative=9325&creativeASIN=1576754057), Meg Wheatley  
  A comprehensive summing up of the thought of one of the most original and creative organizational thinkers of our time.

* [Gracious Space](http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/0975544004/ref=as_li_tf_tl?ie=UTF8&tag=theworldcafe-20&linkCode=as2&camp=1789&creative=9325&creativeASIN=0975544004) by Patricia Hughes  
  Gracious Space is a simple yet powerful approach to working better together. Gracious Space can move organizations and communities forward, together, with deeper understanding and problem solving.

* [Informal Learning](http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/0787981699/ref=as_li_tf_tl?ie=UTF8&tag=theworldcafe-20&linkCode=as2&camp=1789&creative=9325&creativeASIN=0787981699) by Jay Cross  
  This book offers advice on how to support, nurture, and leverage informal learning and helps trainers to go beyond their typical classes and programs.

* [The Complete Guide to Knowledge Management](http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/0470881291/ref=as_li_tf_tl?ie=UTF8&tag=theworldcafe-20&linkCode=as2&camp=1789&creative=9325&creativeASIN=0470881291) by Edna Pasher and Tuvya Ronen  
  A straightforward guide to leveraging your company’s intellectual capital by creating a knowledge management culture.

* [Linked](http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/0452284392/ref=as_li_tf_tl?ie=UTF8&tag=theworldcafe-20&linkCode=as2&camp=1789&creative=9325&creativeASIN=0452284392) by Albert-László Barabási  
  The nation’s foremost expert in the new science of networks, takes us on an intellectual adventure to prove that social networks, corporations, and living organisms are more similar than previously thought.

* [Making Questions Work](http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/0787987271/ref=as_li_tf_tl?ie=UTF8&tag=theworldcafe-20&linkCode=as2&camp=1789&creative=9325&creativeASIN=0787987271) by Dorothy Strachan  
  This book offers over 1700 rich questions that you can borrow or adapt to improve your inquiry skills, and provides clear frameworks that point to when, where, and why particular questions are most useful.

* [Mapping Inner Space](http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1569761388/ref=as_li_tf_tl?ie=UTF8&tag=theworldcafe-20&linkCode=as2&camp=1789&creative=9325&creativeASIN=1569761388) by Nancy Margulies  
  This introduction to visual note taking illustrates how relationships among various concepts are highlighted and more information can be recorded visually on a page.

* [Nature and the Human Soul](http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1577315510/ref=as_li_tf_tl?ie=UTF8&tag=theworldcafe-20&linkCode=as2&camp=1789&creative=9325&creativeASIN=1577315510) by Bill Plotkin  
  Plotkin presents a model for a human life span rooted in the patterns and rhythms of wild nature, a template for individual development that ultimately yields a strategy for cultural transformation.

* [On Dialogue](http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/0415336414/ref=as_li_tf_tl?ie=UTF8&tag=theworldcafe-20&linkCode=as2&camp=1789&creative=9325&creativeASIN=0415336414) by David Bohm  
  This edition serves both as a practical working manual for those interested in engaging in Bohm’s conception of “dialogue” and a deeper exploration of Bohm’s dialogical world view.

* [Power and Love](http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1605093041/ref=as_li_tf_tl?ie=UTF8&tag=theworldcafe-20&linkCode=as2&camp=1789&creative=9325&creativeASIN=1605093041) by Adam Kahane  
  A new approach, proven in the field, for making progress on our most important and difficult collective challenges.

* [The Power of Collective Wisdom and the Trap of Collective Folly](http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1576754456/ref=as_li_tf_tl?ie=UTF8&tag=theworldcafe-20&linkCode=as2&camp=1789&creative=9325&creativeASIN=1576754456) by Alan Briskin, Sheryl Ericson, John Ott, and Tom Callanan  
  An inspired and practical approach to developing the innate power of groups to make wise, compassionate, and creative decisions.

* [Presence](http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/0385516304/ref=as_li_tf_tl?ie=UTF8&tag=theworldcafe-20&linkCode=as2&camp=1789&creative=9325&creativeASIN=0385516304) by Betty Sue Flowers, Otto Scharmer, Jpseph Jaworski. and Peter Senge  
  This year-long series of conversations reveals the human capacity to “presence”—to pre-sense, to become present to an emerging future.

* [The Starfish and the Spider](http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1591841836/ref=as_li_tf_tl?ie=UTF8&tag=theworldcafe-20&linkCode=as2&camp=1789&creative=9325&creativeASIN=1591841836) by Ori Brafman and Rod Beckstrom  
  A pair of Stanford M.B.A.s offer a breezy and entertaining look at how decentralization is changing many organizations.

* [Theory U](http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1576757633/ref=as_li_tf_tl?ie=UTF8&tag=theworldcafe-20&linkCode=as2&camp=1789&creative=9325&creativeASIN=1576757633) by Otto Scharmer  
  By moving through the “U” process we learn to connect to our essential Self in the realm of “presencing”.

* [The Thin Book of Naming Elephants](http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/0966537351/ref=as_li_tf_tl?ie=UTF8&tag=theworldcafe-20&linkCode=as2&camp=1789&creative=9325&creativeASIN=0966537351) by Sue Annis Hammond & Andrea Mayfield  
  This book shows how great companies create an environment that encourages and listens to input from all levels of the organization.

* [Visual Meetings](http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/0470601787/ref=as_li_tf_tl?ie=UTF8&tag=theworldcafe-20&linkCode=as2&camp=1789&creative=9325&creativeASIN=0470601787) by David Sibbet (see also **Visual Teams** and **Visual Leaders**)  
  Visual Meetings explains how anyone can implement powerful visual tools, and how these tools are being used to facilitate both face-to-face and virtual group work.

* [Walk Out Walk On](http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1605097314/ref=as_li_tf_tl?ie=UTF8&tag=theworldcafe-20&linkCode=as2&camp=1789&creative=9325&creativeASIN=1605097314) by Meg Wheatley and Debbie Frieze  
  Provides an intimate experience of how seven healthy and resilient communities took on intractable problems by working together in new and different ways.

---

# **Recommendations** {#recommendations}

**From Sean LeFleur**

* [The 5th Discipline](https://www.amazon.com/Fifth-Discipline-Practice-Learning-Organization/dp/0385517254/ref=sr_1_1?ie=UTF8&qid=1517743115&sr=8-1&keywords=The+5th+Discipline) by Peter Senge (classic in organizational learning from this MIT prof: personal mastery, team learning, mental models, systems thinking, shared vision)

* [The Necessary Revolution](https://www.amazon.com/Necessary-Revolution-Individuals-Organizations-Sustainable/dp/0385519044) by Peter Senge  (how to work together to create a sustainable world)

  * book: [Authentic Leadership: Rediscovering the Secrets to Creating Lasting Value](https://www.amazon.com/Authentic-Leadership-Rediscovering-Secrets-Creating/dp/0787975281/ref=sr_1_1?ie=UTF8&qid=1517780248&sr=8-1&keywords=Authentic+Leadership%3A+Rediscovering+the+Secrets+to+Creating+Lasting+Value) by Bill George

Thaler, Cass R. Sunstein

* [Quiet: The Power of Introverts in a World That Can't Stop Talking](https://www.amazon.com/Quiet-Power-Introverts-World-Talking/dp/0307352153/ref=sr_1_3?s=books&ie=UTF8&qid=1534041491&sr=1-3&keywords=Quiet) by Susan Cain

* [Coaching Skills: The Definitive Guide to Being A Coach](https://www.amazon.com/Coaching-Skills-Definitive-Humanities-Counselling-ebook/dp/B01J8C9204/ref=sr_1_1?keywords=Coaching+Skills+-+Jenny+Rogers&qid=1575166319&s=digital-text&sr=1-1) by Jenny Rogers

* [The Surprising Power of Liberating Structures: Simple Rules to Unleash A Culture of Innovation](https://www.amazon.com/Surprising-Power-Liberating-Structures-Innovation-ebook/dp/B00JET2S76/ref=sr_1_1?keywords=Liberating+Structures&qid=1575166378&s=digital-text&sr=1-1) by Henri Lipmanowicz and Keith McCandless (recommended for meeting/training structural tips for leaders/facilitators)

* [Beyond Reason: Using Emotions as You Negotiate](https://www.amazon.com/Beyond-Reason-Using-Emotions-Negotiate/dp/0143037781/ref=sr_1_1?ie=UTF8&qid=1519728413&sr=8-1&keywords=Beyond+Reason) by Roger Fisher and Daniel Shapiro 

* [Change Your Questions, Change Your Life: 12 Powerful Tools for Leadership, Coaching, and Life](https://www.amazon.com/Change-Your-Questions-Life-Leadership/dp/162656633X/ref=sr_1_2?s=books&ie=UTF8&qid=1534041341&sr=1-2&keywords=Change+Your+Questions%2C+Change+Your+Life) by Marilee Adams Ph.D. and Marshall Goldsmith

* [FYI: For Your Improvement \- Competencies Development Guide](https://www.amazon.com/FYI-Improvement-Competencies-Development-Guide/dp/1933578904/ref=sr_1_1?ie=UTF8&qid=1517743394&sr=8-1&keywords=Korn+Ferry%27s+Competencies+Development+Guide) \- Korn Ferry's Competencies Development Guide

* [The Master and his Emissary: The Divided Brain and the Making of the Western World](https://www.amazon.com/Master-His-Emissary-Divided-Western/dp/0300245920/ref=sr_1_1?keywords=The+Master+and+his+Emissary+by+Iain+McGilchrist&qid=1575173323&s=books&sr=1-1) by Iain McGilchrist

* [The God of the Left Hemisphere: Blake, Bolte Taylor and the Myth of Creation](https://www.amazon.com/God-Left-Hemisphere-Taylor-Creation/dp/1780491018/ref=sr_1_1?keywords=The+God+of+the+Left+Hemisphere+by+Roderick+Tweedy&qid=1575173369&s=books&sr=1-1) by Roderick Tweedy

* [Adaptive Coaching: The Art and Practice of a Client-Centered Approach to Performance Improvement](https://www.amazon.com/Adaptive-Coaching-Client-Centered-Performance-Improvement-ebook/dp/B00969G83Y/ref=sr_1_1?keywords=Adaptive+Coaching%3A+The+Art+and+Practice+of+a+Client-Centered+Approach+to+Performance+Improvement+by+Terry+R.+Bacon&qid=1575173395&s=books&sr=1-1) by Terry R. Bacon and Laurie Voss

Boyce

* [The Leadership Shadow: How to Recognize and Avoid Derailment, Hubris and Overdrive](https://www.amazon.com/Leadership-Shadow-Recognize-Derailment-Overdrive-ebook/dp/B00LZTVRLQ/ref=sr_1_2?keywords=The+leadership+shadow+by+Erik+de+Haan&qid=1575173564&s=books&sr=1-2) by Erik de Haan   
  Good book on blind spots for leaders

**Others**

* [The Big Burn: Teddy Roosevelt and the Fire that Saved America](https://www.amazon.com/Big-Burn-Teddy-Roosevelt-America/dp/0547394608/ref=sr_1_1?keywords=The+Big+Burn%3A+Teddy+Roosevelt+and+the+Fire+that+Saved+America+by+Timothy+Egan&qid=1575123413&sr=8-1) by Timothy Egan  
* [The Hero's Journey: Joseph Campbell on His Life and Work](https://www.amazon.com/Heros-Journey-Joseph-Campbell-Collected/dp/1608681890/ref=sr_1_2?crid=34YT0OM9B7OF&keywords=the+heroes+journey&qid=1562101662&s=gateway&sprefix=usb+c%2Caps%2C183&sr=8-2) by Joseph Campbell  
* [Can't Hurt Me: Master Your Mind and Defy the Odds](https://www.amazon.com/Cant-Hurt-Me-Master-Your/dp/1544512287/ref=sr_1_1?keywords=can%27t+hurt+me&qid=1562019820&s=gateway&sr=8-1) by David Goggins

**From Benjamin P. Hardy, medium.com**

* [As A Man Thinketh](https://www.amazon.com/gp/slredirect/picassoRedirect.html/ref=pa_sp_atf_digital-text_sr_pg1_1?ie=UTF8&adId=A00825109VJALZD5XHZT&url=%2FAs-Man-Thinketh-James-Allen%2Fdp%2F1514698692%2Fref%3Dsr_1_1_sspa%3Fkeywords%3DAs%2BA%2BMan%2BThinketh%26qid%3D1575165478%26s%3Ddigital-text%26sr%3D1-1-spons%26psc%3D1&qualifier=1575165478&id=3153907912891808&widgetName=sp_atf) by James Allen  
  There is no denying it. You are what you think. Your external world is a reflection of who you are, inside. The most honest personal inventory you can take is simple: look at your life. Whether you’re willing to admit it or not, you’ve planned on being where you currently are. Everything thought and decision you’ve made has brought you to this point. You have complete control over your life once you take control of the garden of you mind. What you plant you must reap.

* [Essentialism: The Disciplined Pursuit of Less](https://www.amazon.com/Essentialism-Disciplined-Pursuit-Greg-McKeown-ebook/dp/B00G1J1D28/ref=sr_1_1?keywords=Essentialism%3A+The+Disciplined+Pursuit+of+Less&qid=1575165943&s=digital-text&sr=1-1) by Greg Mckeown   
  Almost everything in life is a distraction. Removing every non-essential element will allow you to be happy, healthy, and productive. This is extremely difficult and requires constant care.  
  Like our minds, our lives are also like a garden. Weeds are continuously popping up, taking us away from those things which matter most. If we don’t continuously prune the garden of our lives, we’ll find we missed the best and most important parts.

* [The Art of Learning: An Inner Journey to Optimal Performance](https://www.amazon.com/Art-Learning-Journey-Optimal-Performance-ebook/dp/B000QCQ970/ref=sr_1_1?keywords=The+Art+of+Learning%3A+An+Inner+Journey+to+Optimal+Performance&qid=1575165906&s=digital-text&sr=1-1) by Josh Waitzkin   
  Becoming the best in the world is not a fluke, but a process. It requires a level of mastery so deep that winning becomes automatic. Don’t seek comfort, but discomfort. Invest in failure — which means getting clobbered by people way better than you. The harder you train in practice, the more successful you’ll be in the game.

* [Relentless: From Good to Great to Unstoppable](https://www.amazon.com/Relentless-Good-Great-Unstoppable/dp/B00R4TQNP6/ref=sr_1_2?keywords=Relentless%3A+From+Good+to+Great+to+Unstoppable&qid=1575165877&s=digital-text&sr=1-2) by Tim S. Grover, Sean Pratt, et al.  
  “From this point, your strategy is to make everyone else get on your level, you’re not going down to theirs. You’re not competing with anyone else, ever again. They’re going to have to compete with you. From now on, the end result is all that matters.” — Tim Grover  
  Being unstoppable is a state-of-mind. In order to be unstoppable, you must act on instinct — with complete trust in yourself. In order to do this, you must block-out all external noise and pressure. You already know what you need to do. Everything you need is already within you. Stop thinking about it \- just do it.

* [The Power of Starting Something Stupid: How to Crush Fear, Make Dreams Happen, and Live without Regret](https://www.amazon.com/Power-Starting-Something-Stupid-without/dp/B00CFK67UU/ref=sr_1_1?keywords=The+Power+of+Starting+Something+Stupid&qid=1575165828&s=digital-text&sr=1-1)  
  by Richie Norton, Natalie Norton, et al.  
  Stupid is the new smart. Every brilliant innovation was once considered a crazy — stupid — idea. Don’t let the fear of looking stupid hold you back from doing your life’s work.

* [The Compound Effect](https://www.amazon.com/Compound-Effect-Darren-Hardy-ebook/dp/B005P1YCNK/ref=sr_1_1?keywords=The+Compound+Effect&qid=1575165795&s=digital-text&sr=1-1) by Darren Hardy    
  How was your day today? If not so good, you’re future isn’t looking so good either.  
  What you do on a daily basis determines everything about your life. Small things become big things. The things you do every day — whether good or bad — compound over time. If you have good habits, your future will explode with exponential goodness. If bad, the opposite.

* [Ender’s Game](https://www.amazon.com/Enders-Game-Ender-Quartet-Book-ebook/dp/B003G4W49C/ref=sr_1_1?keywords=Ender%E2%80%99s+Game&qid=1575165758&s=digital-text&sr=1-1) by Orson Scott Card   
  “In the moment when I truly understand my enemy, understand him well enough to defeat him, then in that very moment I also love him. I think it’s impossible to really understand somebody, what they want, what they believe, and not love them the way they love themselves.”―Orson Scott Card  
  Science fiction is just as essential is non-fiction. This book is my favorite sci-fi. There is an absurd amount of leadership and strategy in this book.

* [Abundance: The Future Is Better Than You Think](https://www.amazon.com/Abundance-Future-Better-Than-Think-ebook/dp/B005FLOGMM/ref=sr_1_1?keywords=Abundance%3A+The+Future+Is+Better+Than+You+Think&qid=1575165733&s=digital-text&sr=1-1) by Peter H. Diamandis and Steven Kotler   
  Want to be a billionaire? Help a billion people. Although an enormous task, thanks to technological advances it’s never been easier. The future is bright for those who consciously contribute to the global good.

* [Rework](https://www.amazon.com/Rework-Jason-Fried-ebook/dp/B002MUAJ2A/ref=sr_1_1?keywords=Rework&qid=1575165694&s=digital-text&sr=1-1) by Jason Fried and David Heinemeier Hansson   
  Don’t get caught up in long-term planning, which is little more than guesswork. Instead, focus on execution and iteration.

* [Zero to One: Notes on Startups, or How to Build the Future](https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/0804139296/ref=as_li_qf_sp_asin_il_tl?ie=UTF8&tag=mannyb-20&camp=1789&creative=9325&linkCode=as2&creativeASIN=0804139296&linkId=8e71ec71305ddb3bf10e1aae2910fb2d) by Peter Theil   
  “All failed companies are the same: they failed to escape competition.”―Peter Thiel  
  Unlike most entrepreneurship books as of late that preach minimum viable products and iterations, Thiel challenges the reader to have definite plans and go big. This book is the dialectical opposite of Rework which is why both books are incredible. Both books are the best I’ve read on the opposite sides of the same coin.

## **Highly Recommended by Others**

* **Increasing** **your impact within organizations:** [Flawless Consulting: A Guide to Getting Your Expertise Used](https://www.amazon.com/Flawless-Consulting-Guide-Getting-Expertise/dp/0470620749/ref=sr_1_1?s=books&ie=UTF8&qid=1534038311&sr=1-1&keywords=+Flawless+Consulting) by Peter Block 

* **Amplify** **the good:** [The Power of Positive Deviance: How Unlikely Innovators Solve the World's Toughest Problems](https://www.amazon.com/Power-Positive-Deviance-Unlikely-Innovators/dp/1422110664/ref=sr_1_1?s=books&ie=UTF8&qid=1534037726&sr=1-1&keywords=The+Power+of+Positive+Deviance) by Richard Pascale, Jerry Sternin and Monique Sternin

* **Creating space to focus on what’s important:** [Deep Work: Rules for Focused Success in a Distracted World](https://www.amazon.com/Deep-Work-Focused-Success-Distracted/dp/1455586692/ref=sr_1_1?s=books&ie=UTF8&qid=1537550034&sr=1-1&keywords=deep+work) by Cal Newport  [review](http://www.wisdomordata.com/blog/2018/1/27/book-recap-deep-work-is-more-valuable-than-ever)   [summary1](https://www.nateliason.com/notes/deep-work-cal-newport)  [summary2](https://sivers.org/book/DeepWork)       [So Good They Can’t Ignore You](https://www.amazon.com/Good-They-Cant-Ignore-You/dp/1455509124/ref=sr_1_1?keywords=So+Good+They+Can%E2%80%99t+Ignore+You+by+Cal+Newport&qid=1558627296&s=gateway&sr=8-1) by Cal Newport [summary](https://www.nateliason.com/notes/good-cant-ignore-cal-newport)

* **Being** **strategic**: [Playing to Win: How Strategy Really Works](https://www.amazon.com/Playing-Win-Strategy-Really-Works-ebook/dp/B00AJVJ1HI/ref=sr_1_1?s=books&ie=UTF8&qid=1534038367&sr=1-1&keywords=Playing+to+Win) by Roger Martin and A.G. Lafley 

* **Scaling** **up your impact**: [Scaling Up Excellence: Getting to More Without Settling for Less](https://www.amazon.com/Scaling-Up-Excellence-Getting-Settling/dp/0385347022/ref=sr_1_1?s=books&ie=UTF8&qid=1534038442&sr=1-1&keywords=Scaling+Up+Excellence) by Bob Sutton and Huggy Rao

* **Being** **more helpful**: [Helping: How to Offer, Give, and Receive Help](https://www.amazon.com/Helping-Offer-Give-Receive-Help/dp/1605098566/ref=sr_1_1?s=books&ie=UTF8&qid=1534038476&sr=1-1&keywords=Helping) by Edgar Schein 

* **Relationship to money:** [The Psychology of Money: Timeless Lessons on Wealth, Greed, and Happiness](https://tinyurl.com/y5eszl2e) by Morgan Housel, Chris Hill, Harriman House 

* **Harnessing neuroscience for personal change**: [Mindsight: The New Science of Personal Transformation](https://www.amazon.com/Mindsight-New-Science-Personal-Transformation/dp/0553386395/ref=sr_1_1?ie=UTF8&qid=1517743313&sr=8-1&keywords=Mindsight+-+Dan+Siegel) by Dan Siegel (a great skill for self-awareness), and [Behave: The Biology of Humans at Our Best and Worst](https://www.amazon.com/Behave-Biology-Humans-Best-Worst-ebook/dp/B01IAUGC5S/ref=sr_1_1?dchild=1&keywords=behave+by+robert&qid=1590605790&sr=8-1) by Robert M. Sapolsky

* **Resilience**: [The Dip: A Little Book That Teaches You When to Quit (and When to Stick)](https://www.amazon.com/Dip-Little-Book-Teaches-Stick-ebook/dp/B000QCSA54/ref=sr_1_5?ie=UTF8&qid=1534038630&sr=8-5&keywords=Seth+Godin) by Seth Godin 

* **Making conflict productive**: [Conflicted: How Productive Disagreements Lead to Better Outcomes](https://tinyurl.com/yz2nl7ot) by Ian Leslie 

* **Living a meaningful life (later in life):** [The 100-Year Life: Living and Working in an Age of Longevity](https://tinyurl.com/yyshx934) by Lynda Gratton, Andrew Scott

* **Understanding that change is a complex system**: [Reinventing Organizations: A Guide to Creating Organizations Inspired by the Next Stage of Human Consciousness](https://www.amazon.com/Reinventing-Organizations-Creating-Inspired-Consciousness-ebook/dp/B00ICS9VI4/ref=sr_1_1?s=books&ie=UTF8&qid=1534038723&sr=1-1&keywords=Reinventing+Organizations) by Frederic Laloux, Ken Wilber

* **Great questions:** [A More Beautiful Question: The Power of Inquiry to Spark Breakthrough Ideas](https://www.amazon.com/More-Beautiful-Question-Inquiry-Breakthrough/dp/1632861054/ref=sr_1_1?s=books&ie=UTF8&qid=1534038760&sr=1-1&keywords=A+More+Beautiful+Question) by Warren Berger, [Making Questions Work](https://www.amazon.com/Making-Questions-Work-Facilitators-Consultants/dp/0787987271/ref=sr_1_1?s=books&ie=UTF8&qid=1534039261&sr=1-1&keywords=Making+Questions+Work) by Dorothy Strachan, [Humble Inquiry](https://www.amazon.com/Humble-Inquiry-Gentle-Instead-Telling/dp/1609949811/ref=pd_sbs_14_1?_encoding=UTF8&pd_rd_i=1609949811&pd_rd_r=94608675-c78d-11e8-9d43-93f44e9c2ed4&pd_rd_w=7f6iT&pd_rd_wg=EwoGA&pf_rd_i=desktop-dp-sims&pf_rd_m=ATVPDKIKX0DER&pf_rd_p=53dead45-2b3d-4b73-bafb-fe26a7f14aac&pf_rd_r=QSTK7DA52BY3J1TB1H3A&pf_rd_s=desktop-dp-sims&pf_rd_t=40701&psc=1&refRID=QSTK7DA52BY3J1TB1H3A) by Edgar H. Schein

* **Learning**: [Make It Stick](https://www.amazon.com/Make-Stick-Peter-C-Brown-ebook/dp/B00JQ3FN7M/ref=sr_1_1?s=books&ie=UTF8&qid=1534038790&sr=1-1&keywords=Make+It+Stick) by Peter Brown, Henry Roediger and Mark McDaniel 

* **Appreciate and marvel at every day, every moments**: [A Short History of Nearly Everything](https://www.amazon.com/Short-History-Nearly-Everything/dp/076790818X/ref=sr_1_1?s=books&ie=UTF8&qid=1534038899&sr=1-1&keywords=A+Short+History+of+Nearly+Everything) by Bill Bryson

* **Saves lives while increasing impact**: [End Malaria](https://www.amazon.com/End-Malaria-Michael-Bungay-Stanier-ebook/dp/B00NLJ52ZU/ref=sr_1_1?s=books&ie=UTF8&qid=1534038914&sr=1-1&keywords=End+Malaria) by Michael Bungay Stanier 

* **Transformational change**: [Leadership from the Inside Out: Becoming a Leader for Life](https://www.amazon.com/Leadership-Inside-Out-Becoming-Leader/dp/1523094354/ref=sr_1_3?s=books&ie=UTF8&qid=1534038932&sr=1-3&keywords=+Leadership+from+the+Inside+Out) by Kevin Cashman, “growing the whole person to grow the whole leader.” "Leadership is authentic influence that creates value." "Involves clarifying our inner identity, purpose, and vision so that our lives thereafter are dedicated to a more conscious, intentional manner of living and leading." "Anyone who is authentically influencing to create value is leading." 

* **Authenticity and enduring value creation**: [Good to Great: Why Some Companies Make the Leap and Others Don't](https://www.amazon.com/Good-Great-Some-Companies-Others/dp/0066620996/ref=sr_1_1?s=books&ie=UTF8&qid=1534038988&sr=1-1&keywords=Good+to+Great) by Jim Collins on Level 5 Leadership 

* **Balancing people effectiveness with results orientation**: [The Extraordinary Leader: Turning Good Managers into Great Leaders](https://www.amazon.com/Extraordinary-Leader-Turning-Managers-Leaders/dp/0071628088/ref=sr_1_1?s=books&ie=UTF8&qid=1534039020&sr=1-1&keywords=The+Extraordinary+Leader) by John Zenger, Joseph Folkman

* **Deepening personal awareness and interpersonal connection**: [Emotional Intelligence: Why It Can Matter More Than IQ](https://www.amazon.com/Emotional-Intelligence-Matter-More-Than/dp/055338371X/ref=sr_1_4?s=books&ie=UTF8&qid=1534039055&sr=1-4&keywords=Emotional+Intelligence), [Primal Leadership](https://www.amazon.com/Primal-Leadership-New-Preface-Authors/dp/1422168034/ref=sr_1_1?s=books&ie=UTF8&qid=1534039179&sr=1-1&keywords=Primal+Leadership), [Working with Emotional Intelligence](https://www.amazon.com/Working-Emotional-Intelligence-Daniel-Goleman/dp/0553378589/ref=sr_1_3?s=books&ie=UTF8&qid=1534039196&sr=1-3&keywords=Working+with+Emotional+Intelligence) by Daniel Goleman, and [Emotional Intelligence 2.0](https://www.amazon.com/Emotional-Intelligence-2-0-Travis-Bradberry/dp/0974320625/ref=as_li_ss_tl?ie=UTF8&qid=1525783202&sr=8-1-spons&keywords=emotional+intelligence+2.0&psc=1&linkCode=sl1&tag=readingraphic-20&linkId=4e533a863ce32def64a0db4191304389) by Bradberry et al  
  * [Emotional Intelligence: Why It Can Matter More Than IQ](https://www.amazon.com/Emotional-Intelligence-Matter-More-Than/dp/055338371X/ref=sr_1_4?s=books&ie=UTF8&qid=1534039055&sr=1-4&keywords=Emotional+Intelligence) provides a basic framework  
  * [Emotional Intelligence 2.0](https://www.amazon.com/Emotional-Intelligence-2-0-Travis-Bradberry/dp/0974320625/ref=as_li_ss_tl?ie=UTF8&qid=1525783202&sr=8-1-spons&keywords=emotional+intelligence+2.0&psc=1&linkCode=sl1&tag=readingraphic-20&linkId=4e533a863ce32def64a0db4191304389) builds on the Goleman’s framework  
  * [Working with Emotional Intelligence](https://www.amazon.com/Working-Emotional-Intelligence-Daniel-Goleman/dp/0553378589/ref=sr_1_3?s=books&ie=UTF8&qid=1534039196&sr=1-3&keywords=Working+with+Emotional+Intelligence) is an anecdotally driven exploration of the concepts

* **Stop Worrying:** [Declutter Your Mind: How to Stop Worrying, Relieve Anxiety, and Eliminate Negative Thinking](https://www.amazon.com/Declutter-Your-Mind-Worrying-Eliminate-ebook/dp/B01KU04K5A/ref=sr_1_6?s=books&ie=UTF8&qid=1534039098&sr=1-6&keywords=How+to+Stop+Worrying) by S.J. Scott and Barrie Davenport

* **Guided Meditations**: [Tarnbrach.com](https://www.tarabrach.com/guided-meditations/) by Tara Brache  
* **Finding Purpose**: [Find Your Why](https://amzn.to/2rJK0dd) by Simon Sinek  
* **Autism**: [How to Be Human: An Autistic Man's Guide to Life](https://tinyurl.com/y44nk4fm) by Jory Fleming, Lyric Winik
